Thank You for Using Our Interface!
The Following List Explains the Use of the Buttons on the Side of the Interface to Make Your Life Easier!
X: This button is used in case you make any mistakes. You can press it and simply start over again
Dist 2 Pts: Click 2 points or type in 2 intersection names. Click this button to get the shortest route between them
Courier: Click on a set of points. Click this button to find the quickest route through all these points. Used by courier companies.
POI range: Click a point or type in an intersection name. Enter a radius. Click this button and you will get all the POIs in that range of the chosen point or intersection
POIs ON: Shows all the POIs on the map as red dots
